# Text Elements
Increase in concentration means More particles per unit volume,
this means that more collisions
can happen per unit time And hence the rate of reaction
would increase ^fnFiT866

An increase in the temperature, The particles would be able
to move more quickly and would have higher kinetic energy,
Causing more particles to collide per unit time
Furthermore a higher proportion of Particles will have activation
energy ^gTasrg8O

A catalyst is a substance that increases the rate of reaction
by reducing the Activation energy. And not changing in the process ^ZX5OTyFR

Steeper line, Or Higher Gradient for Graph 2 and the same
volume of Hydrogen made, Indicates that Copper is catalysing the
reaction ^oWs72AAc

As the reaction goes on, The amount of Reactants decreases
Resulting in less collisions per unit time, And hence the gradient dec ^cZrpPdir
